19.0 OTHER RELEVANT DATA AND INFORMATION 

The Author found no evidence of environmental, social or security concerns on the Jabali 

property although a detailed investigation of these issues was not conducted. As with other 

areas on the La Libertad Concession, B2Gold strives to maintain open and co-operative 

community relations. 

20.0 INTERPRETATION AND CONCLUSIONS 

On March 26, 2009, B2Gold completed a business combination with Central Sun. As a result of 

this transaction, B2Gold acquired the Libertad Mine (100%) and the Limon Mine (95%). B2Gold 

began mining and processing ore from the Crimea and Mojon vein systems on the La Libertad 

Concession in the fourth quarter of 2009 following the completion of the conversion of the 

Libertad Mine from a heap leach mine to a conventional milling operation. From the start of 

commercial production on February 1, 2010, La Libertad produced 68,562 ounces of gold at an 

operating cash cost of $522 per ounce and a total cash cost of $585 per ounce from 1,498,614 

tonnes of ore milled at an average grade of 1.61 g/t gold.  

A geologic review of primary and regional epithermal vein targets with senior Nicaraguan 

geologic staff in 2009 identified several favourable vein targets including the Jabali vein system. 

The Jabali vein structure was partially mined in the past with mining starting in 1862 and 

continuing until the mid 1970s. There are no records of tonnes or grade removed from the mine. 

The Jabali vein structure is located on the eastern part of the La Libertad property near the town 

of Santo Domingo. The Jabali vein system is a low sulphidation epithermal quartz adularia vein 

target hosted by Tertiary aged andesite volcanics. Gold mineralization is associated with quartz 

veins and quartz breccias exhibiting mineralogy and textures characteristic of low sulphidation 

epithermal vein systems. Sulphides are rare as the mineralized structure is oxidized to depths of 

50 to 60 metres at both the Antenna and Central Zones. Fine grained black sulphides and trace 



B2Gold Corp. 
Jabali Project, La Libertad Region, Nicaragua 
NI 43-101 Resource Estimate Technical Report 
 

   
12 May 2011  Page 58  
   
 

amounts of sphalerite, galena and chalcopyrite are noted in drill logs. Anomalous gold grades 

exceeding 1 g/t gold are commonly associated with vuggy and drusy textured quartz breccias. 

In 2009 and 2010, B2Gold completed 31 trenches across the Jabali vein structure over a strike 

length of 3,200 metres. In February 2010, B2Gold began drilling on the Jabali vein structure, 

completing 55 diamond drill holes for 9,659.4 metres. 

Although at an early stage of exploration the drill results to date and continuity of gold grades 

indicate that the Jabali vein is a target of merit and requires additional work to advance it. Based 

on a review of logging, sampling and other data collection and verification procedures, the 

Author has concluded that the geologists on site for B2Gold are doing work that meets or 

exceeds industry standards and the data is valid for resource estimation work.   

In early 2011, an inferred mineral resource estimate was completed by B2Gold on the Jabali 

vein totaling 3.545 million tonnes at a grade 4.58 g/t of gold containing 522,393 ounces of gold. 

The zones remain open to the east, west and to depth. 

RECOMMENDATIONS 

A budget of US$ 8.0 million dollars is recommended for additional exploration and metallurgic 

work on the Jabali structure. The drilling would focus on two objectives; in-fill drilling on the 

Antenna and Central zones to upgrade the inferred resource classification to an indicated 

resource class and continue to drill along strike and test down-dip extensions of the Jabali 

structure to the east and west. In addition, a series of close spaced drill holes (geostat cross) is 

recommended to evaluate short range grade variability along strike and down-dip on the vein 

structure. Metallurgic testing should be initiated to evaluate the recovery characteristics of the 

gold bearing mineralization. 

 

 

 



B2Gold Corp. 
Jabali Project, La Libertad Region, Nicaragua 
NI 43-101 Resource Estimate Technical Report 
 

   
12 May 2011  Page 59

Additional Recommendations within the scope of the proposed 2011 drill campaign include: 

• Additional multi-element ICP analysis and petrographic work to help define 

metallurgic domains for sampling and modeling as well as examine the liberation 

characteristics of the Jabali mineralization. 

• Outline a geotechnical data collection program relevant to open pit and / or 

underground design including: 

1. Structural data for open pit and underground mine design. 

2. Hyrdogeologic data. 

3. Rock Mass Data. 

4. Collect additional density tests in the upper weathered profile.  

• Outline an environmental baseline study of surrounding area.
